people found the following review helpful</div>  <div class="clearboth"></div>  <div class="mt4 ttl"><span class="swSprite s_star_5_0 " title="5.0 out of 5 stars" ><span>5.0 out of 5 stars</span></span>   <a href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R138GOQNGXAE1P/ref=cm_cr_dp_title?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00GU4F4OM&nodeID=468642&store=videogames" class="txtlarge gl3 gr4 reviewTitle valignMiddle"><strong>Mammoth in quality</strong></a><span class="gry valignMiddle">         <span class="inlineblock txtsmall">March 25, 2014</span> </span></div>  <div class="mt4 ath"><span class="gr10">             <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/AAVWNRRJCAT3N/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp" class="noTextDecoration">Isreal Alexander</a></span> </span>   </div>  <div class="txtsmall mt4 fvavp"><span class="inlineblock avpOrVine" ><span class="orange strong avp">Verified Purchase</span></span></div>  <div class="mt9 reviewText">       <div class="drkgry">   <span class="MHRHead">PROS:<br />This mouse far surpassed my expectations. It makes my old G5 look like a cheap knockoff.<br /><br />Construction: The material is very similar to the Logitech (a little rough, textured...very grippy without being uncomfortable) and doesn't seem to be a magnet for oils/dirt. The braided cable is very well built, with reinforcement at the mouse end (to prevent it from eventually fraying there from the constant bending, as my G5 eventually did) and USB end. There is also a Velcro strap on the cord for easy storage or just keeping the cable shorter for laptop use. The mouse seems to have very tight tolerances; it doesn't creak when you hold it tightly or flex at all, the button actions are all very crisp and consistent, the mouse wheel is very smooth and has individual clicks when scrolling, and there are 4 well placed &#34;extra&#34; buttons (aside from normal left/right click, mouse wheel, and DPI buttons) that are customizable.<br /><br />Use: It tracks on virtually anything, is nice and slick to move around thanks to the huge Teflon pads (but heavy enough with the included weights to be stable), has a massive range of DPI settings, selectable on the go (5 preprogrammed settings, with total control available in the included software), and overall just feels like a high quality mouse that should be a pleasure to use for years to come.<br /><br />Software: The software is pretty comprehensive. It allows macros to be created/assigned, full control over DPI/lighting (color, speed and flashing or &#34;breathing&#34; intensity)/pointer speed/acceleration/double-click speed/polling rate/etc, has 5 profiles you can customize and load, and is an easy install.<br /><br />CONS:<br />Not much to say here.</span><span class="MHRRest" style="display:none"> The software does not include &#34;double-click&#34; as a selectable mouse button function (I like to keep a double-click button assigned for certain games) but you can bypass that with a quick double-click macro. Also, the mouse wheel does not side-scroll, tho personally I don't care either way.<br /><br />CONCLUSION:<br />Awesome product! Would gladly pay full retail for it, and considering I saved over 50% off that, I am looking for a 6th star to rate it with. Highly recommended.</span> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Redragon-Mammoth-Precision-Programmable-Cartridge-Switches/product-reviews/B00GU4F4OM/ref=cm_cr_dp_text?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=0&sortBy=byRankDescending#R138GOQNGXAE1P"        <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A3JR30GUUDW9NF/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp" class="noTextDecoration">A. Moore</a></span> </span>   </div>  <div class="txtsmall mt4 fvavp"><span class="inlineblock avpOrVine" ><span class="orange strong avp">Verified Purchase</span></span></div>  <div class="mt9 reviewText">       <div class="drkgry">   <span class="MHRHead">I had got a gaming mouse along with a gaming laptop, that I had built online. I loved the gaming mouse I had but due to its cheap rubber wire, the connection at the USB plug began to come loose so I had to retire it. The gaming mouse I had, had a decent weight to it which I loved and it was a bit smaller than this one, but as a female it felt fine for me. I don't play any extreme online gaming where I have to worry about any extreme use but I did want something durable and nice enough for me.<br /><br />So far I really like the feel of this mouse. It is a bit bigger than the one I had but not so big that its uncomfortable for me. I'm able to rest my palm on it without an issue even if my fingers have to be spread over it a whole lot more than my other mouse. Also the texture did feel odd to me at first, kind of a very light grainy texture but not something that's too hard to get use to.<br /><br />My main reasons for buying it was the threaded cover for the cord, and I couldn't get myself to go for a wireless mouse. There always seems to be complaints about delays and again I don't play extreme shooting games or anything along the lines where a delay now and then would be a big issue but Id prefer not to have any of it either way. Even if a mouse with a cord might seem a bit tedious, as if the cord might get in the way, but I don't mind. I would prefer smooth, clean movements without having to guess when it might freeze.<br /><br />Another thing I really love about this mouse is the light up colors and the fact you can change them. But that's more of a small plus than a need but I enjoy it very much, and it doesn't seem to be too distracting for me.<br /><br />The mouse glides with ease, the buttons and wheel feels secure and it all fits my needs so far.</span><span class="MHRRest" style="display:none"> I do play games, at least two different ones a day from Left 4 Dead 2, Thief, FF XIV and many others, all different in style from RPG and etc. I also work with CS6 for graphic design and a few other similar programs like it. This mouse meets me expectations and more....if anything does change I will make sure to update my review, but so far I am loving this mouse.</span> <a valignMiddle"><strong>Almost perfect!</strong></a><span class="gry valignMiddle">        <span class="inlineblock txtsmall">May 22, 2014</span> </span></div>  <div class="mt4 ath"><span class="gr10">        <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A1U21ZIXJK3FF7/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp" class="noTextDecoration">Jonathan Hayes</a></span> </span>   </div>  <div class="txtsmall mt4 fvavp"><span class="inlineblock avpOrVine" ><span class="orange strong avp">Verified Purchase</span></span></div>  <div class="mt9 reviewText">       <div class="drkgry">   <span class="MHRHead">FIRST OFF, i'm not being paid for this review.. you can verify im real at facebook.com/hayes88 or anywhere else u want me to lol.<br /><br />Okay, I just got this mouse. Only took a couple days to get here. The packaging was nice.<br /><br />The feel - The texture of the black actually feels really nice. The buttons are easy to click, and it fits my hand size just perfectly. I don't have a huge or small hand, it's pretty medium sized. It also moves very nice on the mouse pad.<br /><br />The weight - It comes with the weights already inside the mouse. It should've came with the weights outside of it, and made the weights a little heavier. Not to make it sound like the mouse is too light, but you have to use all of the weights to make it just good enough. So it's good on the weight.<br /><br />The software - The software looks really nice and professionally made, and has a lot of features. This is the only thing that had a slight drawback for me, but it's not worth ditching the mouse over. There needs to be finer control over the DPI and mouse speed, as well as the lighting. It's not too bad though and you can most likely still find the right mouse speed you'd like, and with some extra work the lighting you want.<br /><br />The lights - The lights in the mouse are pretty nice. Going back to the software drawback, it doesn't have enough control over the lights in the software. In the lights menu, it only lets you customize the logo light and the two back lights. The forward light colors, and the light brightness on the bottom is preset to every profile and can't be changed.</span><span class="MHRRest" style="display:none"> So if you want to change it to a blue light for example and bright lights on the bottom, you'd have to set it to that profile and re-configure all of the buttons and DPI/speed for that profile, as well as the colors in the back to match. It's a bit of a headache, but it can be done in less then 5 min. Not a huge deal i guess.<br /><br />The cable - couldnt get any better as far as the way its made and how it looks.<br /><br />The buttons - they're all in the right spot. Anywhere else and it would screw things up.</span> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Redragon-Mammoth-Precision-Programmable-Cartridge-Switches/product-reviews/B00GU4F4OM/ref=cm_cr_dp_text?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=0&sortBy=byRankDescending#RUS5X9B1HMNX9" class="MHRExpandLink readMoreLink">Read more &rsaquo;</a> </div>  </div>  <div class="imageTiles" style="margin-top:5px">   </div>  <div class="clearboth txtsmall gt9 vtStripe">    <div class="fl
